# <a name="dimensions-and-measurements-available-in-call-quality-dashboard-cqd"></a><span data-ttu-id="5ebce-103">Dimensioni e misure disponibili in Call Quality Dashboard (CQD)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-103">Dimensions and measurements available in Call Quality Dashboard (CQD)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-104">Il call quality dashboard (CQD) per Microsoft Teams e Skype for Business online consente di comprendere meglio la qualità delle chiamate effettuate con questi servizi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-104">The Call Quality Dashboard (CQD) for Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business Online allows you to better understand call quality of calls made with these services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-105">Questo argomento fornisce informazioni dettagliate sulle dimensioni e le misure visibili tramite CQD.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-105">This topic provides detailed information about the dimensions and measurements visible through CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-106">Per altre informazioni su CQD, vedere Usare [CQD](quality-of-experience-review-guide.md)per gestire la qualità delle chiamate e delle riunioni in Microsoft Teams.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-106">To learn more about CQD, see [Use CQD to manage call and meeting quality in Microsoft Teams](quality-of-experience-review-guide.md).</span></span>

## <a name="first-and-second-endpoint-classification"></a><span data-ttu-id="5ebce-107">Classificazione del primo e secondo endpoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-107">First and Second endpoint classification</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-108">Molte delle dimensioni e delle misure in CQD sono etichettate come prima o seconda.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-108">Many of the dimensions and measurements in CQD are labeled as first or second.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-109">La seguente logica determina quale endpoint coinvolto nello stream o chiamata viene etichettato come primo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-109">The following logic determines which endpoint involved in the stream or call is labeled as first:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-110">Un endpoint del server (MCU AV, Mediation Server e così via) viene considerato prima di tutto quando un server è coinvolto nello stream o nella chiamata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-110">A Server endpoint (AV MCU, Mediation Server, and so on) is considered First when a Server is involved in the stream or call.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-111">Un endpoint client viene considerato Second a meno che lo stream non sia compreso tra due endpoint server.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-111">A Client endpoint is considered Second unless the stream is between two Server endpoints.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-112">Se entrambi gli endpoint sono dello stesso tipo, il primo e il secondo sono impostati in base all'ordinamento interno della categoria agente utente per garantire che l'ordinamento sia coerente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-112">If both endpoints are the same type, first vs. second is set based on internal ordering of the user agent category to ensure that the ordering is consistent.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-113">Ad esempio, qui ogni riga rappresenta una coppia di agenti utente coinvolti in un flusso:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-113">For example, here each row represents a pair of User Agents involved in a stream:</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-p103">Questa classificazione primo-secondo è distinta da quale endpoint sia il chiamante o il chiamato. La dimensione Il primo è il chiamante può essere usata per aiutare a individuare quale endpoint è il chiamante o il chiamato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-p103">That First and Second classification is separate from which endpoint is the caller or callee. The First Is Caller dimension can be used to help identify which endpoint was the caller or callee.</span></span>

## <a name="dimensions"></a><span data-ttu-id="5ebce-155">Dimensioni</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-155">Dimensions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-156">Le informazioni sulle dimensioni si basano in parte sui dati caricati nel portale CQD.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-156">Dimensions information is based in part on data uploaded to the CQD portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-157">Molti valori di quota possono essere usati anche come filtri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-157">Many Dimension values can also be used as filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-158">La tabella seguente elenca le dimensioni attualmente disponibili in CQD, nell'ordine indicato nell'editor di query usato per creare report o modificare report definiti in precedenza.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-158">The following table lists the dimensions currently available in CQD, in the order listed in the Query Editor used to create reports or edit previously defined reports.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2539">Packet Loss Rate</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2539">Packet Loss Rate</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2540">Percentuale</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2540">Percentage</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2541">Percentuale di flussi tra Mediation Server e SBC o Gateway, se disponibile.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2541">The percentage of streams between Mediation Server and SBC or Gateway, if available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2542">Per altre [informazioni, vedere Classificazione dei flussi nel dashboard della qualità](stream-classification-in-call-quality-dashboard.md) delle chiamate.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2542">Please see [Stream Classification in Call Quality Dashboard](stream-classification-in-call-quality-dashboard.md) for more information.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2543">**Esempio:** 1,2%</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2543">**Example:** 1.2%</span></span>||
|<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2544">Latenza (tempo di andata e ritorno)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2544">Latency (Round-trip Time)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2545">Millisecondi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2545">Milliseconds</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2546">Tempo medio di round trip di propagazione della rete per flusso calcolato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2546">The average network propagation round-trip time per stream computed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2547">Per altre [informazioni, vedere Classificazione dei flussi nel dashboard della qualità](stream-classification-in-call-quality-dashboard.md) delle chiamate.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2547">Please see [Stream Classification in Call Quality Dashboard](stream-classification-in-call-quality-dashboard.md) for more information.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2548">**Esempio:** 3,49</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2548">**Example:** 3.49</span></span>||

### <a name="notes-on-dimension-data-typeunits"></a><span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2559">Note sul tipo/unità di dati delle dimensioni</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2559">Notes on dimension data type/units</span></span>

#### <a name="boolean"></a><span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2560">Boolean</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2560">Boolean</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2561">I valori booleani sono sempre True o False.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2561">Boolean values are always either True or False.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2562">In alcuni casi, True può essere rappresentato anche come 1 e False come 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2562">In some cases, True can also be represented as 1 and False can be represented as 0.</span></span>

#### <a name="range"></a><span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2563">Intervallo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2563">Range</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2564">Le dimensioni fornite come intervallo o gruppo di valori sono indicate utilizzando il formato seguente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2564">Dimensions that are provided as range or group of values are shown using the following format:</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2565">_\<sort order string\> [\<lower bound inclusive\> - \<upper bound exclusive\>_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2565">_\<sort order string\> [\<lower bound inclusive\> - \<upper bound exclusive\>_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2566">Ad esempio, la dimensione Durata (Minuti) rappresenta la durata della chiamata in secondi e il valore è riferito come intervallo di valori.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2566">For example, the Duration (Minutes) dimension represents the call duration in seconds with the value reported as a range of values.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2567">Duration (Minutes)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2567">Duration (Minutes)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2568">Interpretazione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2568">How to interpret</span></span> |
|:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2569">062: [0 - 0)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2569">062: [0 - 0)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2570">Durata flusso = 0 minuti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2570">Stream duration = 0 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2571">064: [1 - 2)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2571">064: [1 - 2)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2572">1 minuto < = durata flusso < 2 minuti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2572">1 minute < = stream duration < 2 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2573">065: [2 - 3)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2573">065: [2 - 3)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2574">2 minuti < = durata flusso < 3 minuti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2574">2 minutes < = stream duration < 3 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2575">066: [3–4)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2575">066: [3–4)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2576">3 minuti < = durata flusso < 4 minuti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2576">3 minutes < = stream duration < 4 minutes</span></span> |
|  | |

<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-p316">La stringa \<sort order string> si usa per controllare l'ordinamento quando si presentano i dati e si può utilizzare per filtrare. Ad esempio, un filtro su Durata (Minuti) < "065", mostrerà flussi con una durata inferiore a 2 minuti (lo "0" iniziale è necessario perché il filtro funzioni come previsto).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-p316">The \<sort order string> is used to control the sort order when presenting the data and can be used for filtering. For example, a filter on Duration (Minutes) < "065", would show streams with duration less than 2 minutes (The leading '0' is needed for the filter to work as expected).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2579">Il valore effettivo della stringa di ordinamento non è significativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2579">The actual value of the sort order string isn't significant.</span></span>

#### <a name="enumeration-strings"></a><span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2580">Stringhe di enumerazione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2580">Enumeration strings</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2581">Le stringhe usate da CQD sono spesso derivate da file di dati e possono essere quasi qualsiasi combinazione di caratteri entro la lunghezza consentita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2581">Strings used by CQD are often derived from data files, and these can be nearly any combination of character within the allowed length.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2582">Alcune dimensioni hanno l'aspetto di stringhe, ma poiché possono essere solo uno di un breve elenco di valori predefiniti, sono enumerazioni e non stringhe vere.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2582">Some dimensions look like strings, but since they can only be one of a short list of predefined values, they are enumerations and not true strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2583">Alcune stringhe di enumerazione vengono usate anche in coppie.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2583">Some enumerations strings are also used in pairs.</span></span>

#### <a name="enumeration-pair"></a><span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2584">Coppia di enumerazione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2584">Enumeration pair</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2585">Le dimensioni fornite come coppia di enumerazione sono indicate utilizzando il formato seguente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2585">Dimensions that are provided as an enumeration pair are shown using the following format:</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2586">_\<enumeration value from one end point\> : \<enumeration value from the other endpoint\>_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2586">_\<enumeration value from one end point\> : \<enumeration value from the other endpoint\>_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2587">L'ordinamento dei valori di enumerazione è coerente ma non riflette l'ordinamento del primo e del secondo endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2587">The ordering of the enumeration values is consistent but doesn't reflect ordering of the first or second endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2588">Ad esempio, la coppia dettagli di connessione di rete mostra i valori dei dettagli di connessione di rete dei due endpoint:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2588">For example, the Network Connection Detail Pair shows the Network Connection Detail values for the two endpoints:</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2589">Network Connection Detail Pair</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2589">Network Connection Detail Pair</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2590">Interpretazione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2590">How to interpret</span></span> |
|:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2591">Cablata : Cablata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2591">Wired : Wired</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2592">Il primo e il secondo endpoint usavano entrambi connessioni ethernet cablate.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2592">First and second endpoints both used wired ethernet connections.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2593">Cablata : WiFi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2593">Wired : wifi</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2594">Il primo endpoint usava una connessione ethernet cablata mentre il secondo endpoint usava una connessione WiFi oppure il secondo endpoint usava una connessione ethernet cablata mentre il primo endpoint usava una connessione WiFi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2594">First endpoint used wired ethernet connection and second endpoint used Wi-Fi connection, or the second endpoint used wired ethernet connection and first endpoint used Wi-Fi connection.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2595">: WiFi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2595">: wifi</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2596">Il primo endpoint usava una connessione WiFi e la connessione di rete usata dal secondo endpoint era sconosciuta oppure il secondo endpoint usava una connessione WiFi e la connessione di rete usata dal primo endpoint era sconosciuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2596">First endpoint used a WiFi connection and the network connection used by the second endpoint is unknown, or the second endpoint used a WiFi connection and the network connection used by the first endpoint is unknown.</span></span> |
| | |

#### <a name="blank-values"></a><span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2597">Valori vuoti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2597">Blank values</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2598">Nella tabella sopra riportata sono elencati i motivi possibili per cui una dimensione potrebbe essere vuota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2598">The table above lists possible reasons why a dimension may be blank.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2599">Molte dimensioni e misure saranno vuote se la dimensione Record QoE disponibile è falsa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2599">Many dimensions and measurements will be blank if the QoE Record Available dimension is false.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-2600">In genere questa situazione si verifica quando non è stato possibile effettuare la chiamata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-2600">This typically occurs when the call wasn't successfully established.</span></span>

### <a name="notes-on-measurements"></a><span data-ttu-id="5ebce-3226">Note sulle misure</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-3226">Notes on measurements</span></span>

#### <a name="accuracy-limitations"></a><span data-ttu-id="5ebce-3227">Limitazioni di accuratezza</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-3227">Accuracy limitations</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-3228">Alcune misurazioni del numero di utenti e chiamate si basano sull'esecuzione di un'operazione countif distinta sul set di dati per calcolare il conteggio.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-3228">Certain user and call count measurements rely on performing a distinct countif operation on the data set to compute the count.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-3229">Attualmente si verifica un errore fino a 0,2% inerente all'operazione countif distinta a seconda del numero di righe su cui viene eseguita l'operazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-3229">There is currently an up to 0.2% error inherent with the distinct countif operation depending on the number of rows the operation is performed on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-3230">Per ottenere il volume più accurato, è consigliabile usare le misure di conteggio dei flussi perché non si basano su questa operazione countif distinta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-3230">For the most accurate volume, you should use stream count measures since they do not rely on this distinct countif operation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-3231">L'applicazione di filtri per ridurre il volume di dati può ridurre l'errore, ma non eliminare questa fonte di errore in chiamate distinte e conteggi degli utenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-3231">Filtering to reduce the data volume may reduce the error but may not eliminate this source of error in distinct call and user counts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-3232">Per altre informazioni su questa limitazione, vedere la [funzione di aggregazione dcount](/azure/data-explorer/kusto/query/dcount-aggfunction).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-3232">More information about this limitation can be found here [dcount aggregate function](/azure/data-explorer/kusto/query/dcount-aggfunction).</span></span>

## <a name="filters"></a><span data-ttu-id="5ebce-3233">Filtri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-3233">Filters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5ebce-3234">Molti valori di Dimensione e Misura possono essere usati anche come filtri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-3234">Many Dimension and Measurement values can also be used as filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5ebce-3235">È possibile usare i filtri nella query per eliminare le informazioni nello stesso modo in cui si seleziona una dimensione o una misura per aggiungere o includere informazioni nella query.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5ebce-3235">You can use filters in your query to eliminate information in the same way you'd select a Dimension or Measurement to add or include information in the query.</span></span>
